**ClawHub SKILL.md æ ¸å¿ƒç»“æ„**ï¼š

```yaml
name: nox-influencer
description: AI-powered influencer marketing automation for brands

  - name: search
    description: Discover creators across YouTube, TikTok, and Instagram. Check your memory for past search preferences first.
  - name: analyze
    description: Deep analysis of a creator's profile and authenticity
  - name: outreach
    description: Send personalized outreach emails to creators. Call campaigns first for context.
  - name: negotiate
    description: Negotiate collaboration pricing with creators
  - name: campaigns
    description: Create campaigns and view collaboration history. Use this FIRST to set context or recall past work.

  type: api_key
  env: KOL_API_KEY
```

**ChatGPT GPT Action**ï¼šåŸºäº REST API å±‚çš„ OpenAPI 3.1 spec è‡ªåŠ¨ç”Ÿæˆï¼Œè¦†ç›– 5 ä¸ª Day 1 Toolã€‚

#### 2.4.1 SKILL.md å®Œæ•´è§„èŒƒ

**å‚æ•°ä¼ é€’**ï¼šCLI å‚æ•°æ ¼å¼æ˜ å°„

```bash
# discover_creators
nox search "US beauty TikTokers 10K-1M followers"
nox search --platform tiktok --country US --niche beauty --followers 10000-1000000

# analyze_creator
nox analyze @beautybyjess --deep
nox analyze --url "https://tiktok.com/@beautybyjess"

# outreach_creators
nox outreach @beautybyjess @glowwithme --brief "protein powder launch" --preview
nox outreach @beautybyjess @glowwithme --brief "protein powder launch" --send

# negotiate
nox negotiate @beautybyjess --max 900 --target 800 --preview
nox negotiate @beautybyjess --max 900 --target 800 --start

# manage_campaigns
nox campaigns create --name "Q1 Beauty" --brief "è›‹ç™½ç²‰æ¨å¹¿"
nox campaigns
nox campaigns --id cmp_001
nox campaigns --creator @beautybyjess
```

**é”™è¯¯å¤„ç†**ï¼šexit code æ ‡å‡†

| Exit Code | å«ä¹‰ | ç¤ºä¾‹ |
|:---------:|------|------|
| 0 | æˆåŠŸ | æ­£å¸¸è¿”å›ç»“æœ |
| 1 | ä¸šåŠ¡é”™è¯¯ï¼ˆç”¨æˆ·å¯ä¿®å¤ï¼‰ | credit ä¸è¶³ã€å‚æ•°ç¼ºå¤±ã€è¾¾äººæœªæ‰¾åˆ° |

**stderr è¾“å‡º**ï¼šé”™è¯¯ä¿¡æ¯è¾“å‡ºåˆ° stderrï¼ˆä¸æ±¡æŸ“ stdout çš„ JSON è¾“å‡ºï¼‰ï¼ŒAgent å¯åˆ†åˆ«å¤„ç†ã€‚

#### 2.4.2 GPT Action å®Œæ•´è§„èŒƒ

**è®¤è¯æ–¹æ¡ˆ**ï¼šAPI Key via `Authorization: Bearer` headerï¼ˆä¸ç”¨ OAuthï¼Œé™ä½å¤æ‚åº¦ï¼‰ã€‚

**OpenAPI 3.1 Spec ç¤ºä¾‹**ï¼ˆdiscover_creatorsï¼‰ï¼š

```yaml
openapi: 3.1.0
info:
  title: NoxInfluencer
  version: 1.0.0
  description: AI-powered influencer marketing automation for brands
servers:
  - url: https://api.noxinfluencer.com/v1
paths:
  /tools/discover_creators:
    post:
      operationId: discoverCreators
      summary: Search and discover influencers across YouTube, TikTok, and Instagram
      security:
        - bearerAuth: []
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/DiscoverCreatorsInput'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Successful search results
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/DiscoverCreatorsOutput'
        '400':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/BadRequest'
        '402':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/InsufficientCredits'
        '429':
          $ref: '#/components/responses/RateLimited'
components:
  securitySchemes:
    bearerAuth:
      type: http
      scheme: bearer
  responses:
    BadRequest:
      description: Invalid parameters
      content:
        application/json:
          schema:
            $ref: '#/components/schemas/ErrorResponse'
    InsufficientCredits:
      description: Not enough credits
      content:
        application/json:
          schema:
            $ref: '#/components/schemas/ErrorResponse'
    RateLimited:
      description: Too many requests
      content:
        application/json:
          schema:
            $ref: '#/components/schemas/ErrorResponse'
```

> MCP 2025-06 è§„èŒƒå·²åºŸå¼ƒ SSEï¼Œç»Ÿä¸€ä½¿ç”¨ Streamable HTTPã€‚ä¸¤ç§ä¼ è¾“æ¨¡å¼ä»åŒä¸€ä»£ç åº“æ„å»ºã€‚

**è´¨é‡ä¸å‘å¸ƒ**ï¼šMCP Server ä»£ç  < 500 è¡Œç›®æ ‡ï¼Œsemver ç‰ˆæœ¬ç®¡ç†ï¼Œå‘å¸ƒå‰è‡ªåŠ¨æ ¡éªŒï¼ˆlint + æµ‹è¯• + å®‰å…¨å®¡è®¡ï¼‰ï¼Œbeta â†’ éªŒè¯ â†’ æ­£å¼ releaseã€‚

**CLI å‘½ä»¤å¯¹ç…§**ï¼š

```bash
# discover_creators
nox search "US beauty TikTokers 10K-1M followers"
nox search --platform tiktok --country US --niche beauty --followers 10000-1000000

# analyze_creator
nox analyze @beautybyjess --deep
nox analyze --url "https://tiktok.com/@beautybyjess"

# outreach_creators
nox outreach @beautybyjess @glowwithme --brief "protein powder launch" --preview
nox outreach @beautybyjess @glowwithme --brief "protein powder launch" --send

# negotiate
nox negotiate @beautybyjess --max 900 --target 800 --preview
nox negotiate @beautybyjess --max 900 --target 800 --start

# manage_campaigns
nox campaigns create --name "Q1 Beauty" --brief "è›‹ç™½ç²‰æ¨å¹¿"
nox campaigns
nox campaigns --id cmp_001
nox campaigns --creator @beautybyjess
```

**CLI å¯ç»„åˆæ€§**ï¼ˆAgent ç¼–æ’ä¼˜åŠ¿ï¼‰ï¼š


#### 3.6.1 èšæ˜Ÿå·²æœ‰èƒ½åŠ›ï¼ˆServices å±‚å¤ç”¨ï¼‰

#### 3.6.2 Services å±‚æ¥å£å®šä¹‰

NoxInfluencer Core å±‚é€šè¿‡ä»¥ä¸‹æ¥å£æ¶ˆè´¹èšæ˜Ÿé‚®ä»¶èƒ½åŠ›ï¼ˆæ¥å£å®šä¹‰åœ¨ Coreï¼Œå®ç°åœ¨ Servicesï¼‰ï¼š

```typescript
// Core å±‚å®šä¹‰çš„æ¥å£ï¼ˆæ¥å£å®šä¹‰åœ¨ Coreï¼Œå®ç°åœ¨ Servicesï¼‰
interface EmailService {
  // æ‰¹é‡å‘é€ï¼šCore ç”Ÿæˆé‚®ä»¶å†…å®¹ï¼ŒServices è´Ÿè´£ä¼ è¾“
  batchSend(emails: OutboundEmail[]): Promise<SendResult[]>

  // æŸ¥è¯¢æŠ•é€’çŠ¶æ€
  getDeliveryStatus(messageIds: string[]): Promise<DeliveryStatus[]>
}

// Core å±‚å®šä¹‰çš„ LLM æ¨ç†æ¥å£ï¼ˆä¸ EmailService åŒä¸º DI æ³¨å…¥çš„ Services æ¥å£ï¼‰
interface LLMService {
  // è‡ªç„¶è¯­è¨€â†’ç»“æ„åŒ–æŸ¥è¯¢ã€é‚®ä»¶å†…å®¹ç”Ÿæˆã€è°ˆåˆ¤ç­–ç•¥æ¨ç†
  complete(prompt: string, options?: LLMOptions): Promise<string>
}

// è°ˆåˆ¤çŠ¶æ€æœºçš„å›å¤å¤„ç†ï¼ˆCore å±‚çº¯å‡½æ•°ï¼ŒShell å±‚è°ƒåº¦ï¼‰
// Shell å±‚æ¥æ”¶å›å¤äº‹ä»¶åè°ƒç”¨æ­¤å‡½æ•°ï¼ŒCore å±‚ä¸ä¸»åŠ¨è®¢é˜…äº‹ä»¶
interface NegotiationEngine {
  processReply(negotiationId: string, reply: InboundEmail): NegotiationAction
}

interface OutboundEmail {
  to: string                    // è¾¾äººé‚®ç®±
  from_account?: string         // æŒ‡å®šå‘é€è´¦å·ï¼ˆå¯é€‰ï¼Œé»˜è®¤è‡ªåŠ¨åˆ†é…ï¼‰
  subject: string
  html_body: string             // Core å±‚ AI ç”Ÿæˆçš„é‚®ä»¶å†…å®¹
  text_body: string             // çº¯æ–‡æœ¬å›é€€
  reply_to: string              // å›å¤åœ°å€ï¼ˆç”¨äºå›å¤æ£€æµ‹ï¼‰
  metadata: {
    brand_id: string
    creator_id: string
    campaign_id?: string
    email_type: 'outreach' | 'negotiation' | 'follow_up'
  }
}

interface DeliveryStatus {
  message_id: string
  status: 'queued' | 'sent' | 'delivered' | 'opened' | 'clicked' | 'replied' | 'bounced' | 'failed'
  updated_at: string
}

interface InboundEmail {
  message_id: string            // å…³è”çš„åŸå§‹å‘é€ message_id
  from: string                  // è¾¾äººå›å¤é‚®ç®±
  subject: string
  body: string
  received_at: string
}

// Core å±‚çº¯å‡½æ•°è¿”å›å€¼ï¼šæŒ‡ç¤º Shell å±‚æ‰§è¡Œçš„ä¸‹ä¸€æ­¥åŠ¨ä½œ
type NegotiationAction =
  | { action: 'send_counter'; email: OutboundEmail }    // å‘é€ä¸‹ä¸€è½®æŠ¥ä»·
  | { action: 'agreed'; confirmation_draft: string }     // è¾¾æˆä¸€è‡´
  | { action: 'stalled'; reason: string }                // è¶…è½®æ¬¡æš‚åœ
  | { action: 'rejected'; reason: string }               // è¾¾äººæ‹’ç»
  | { action: 'over_budget'; last_quote: number }        // è¶…é¢„ç®—ç»ˆæ­¢
```

#### 3.6.3 æ¶æ„è¾¹ç•Œï¼ˆå…³é”®çº¦æŸï¼‰

| å±‚ | è´Ÿè´£ | ä¸è´Ÿè´£ |
|----|------|-------|
| **Shell** | æ¥æ”¶å›å¤äº‹ä»¶ï¼Œè°ƒç”¨ Core çš„ `processReply()` è·å–ä¸‹ä¸€æ­¥åŠ¨ä½œï¼Œæ‰§è¡ŒåŠ¨ä½œï¼ˆå‘é€é‚®ä»¶/æ›´æ–°çŠ¶æ€ï¼‰ | é‚®ä»¶å†…å®¹ç”Ÿæˆã€è°ˆåˆ¤ç­–ç•¥ã€å‘é€æ—¶æœºå†³ç­– |
| **Core** | é‚®ä»¶å†…å®¹ç¼–æ’ï¼ˆé€šè¿‡ LLMService DIï¼‰ã€é‚€çº¦ç­–ç•¥ã€è°ˆåˆ¤çŠ¶æ€æœºï¼ˆçº¯å‡½æ•° `processReply` â†’ `NegotiationAction`ï¼‰ã€å‘é€æ—¶æœºå†³ç­– | å‘é€é€šé“é€‰æ‹©ã€é¢‘æ§ã€æŠ•é€’è¿½è¸ªå®ç°ã€äº‹ä»¶ç›‘å¬ |
| **Servicesï¼ˆèšæ˜Ÿé‚®ä»¶ï¼‰** | SMTP/API å‘é€ã€è´¦å·æ± è½®è½¬ã€é¢‘æ§ã€æŠ•é€’è¿½è¸ªã€å›å¤æ£€æµ‹ã€ååƒåœ¾ | é‚®ä»¶å†…å®¹ç”Ÿæˆã€ä¸šåŠ¡æµç¨‹ç¼–æ’ã€å‘é€ç­–ç•¥ |

### å‰ç½®çº¢çº¿ï¼ˆå¼€å·¥å‰å¿…é¡»å®Œæˆï¼‰â€” å…¨éƒ¨é€šè¿‡

**H4 èšæ˜Ÿæ•°æ®è´¨é‡éªŒè¯** âœ… å·²å®Œæˆï¼ˆ2026-02ï¼‰

éªŒè¯ç»“è®ºï¼šèšæ˜Ÿæ•°æ®è¦†ç›–ç‡ã€æ–°é²œåº¦ã€å‡†ç¡®åº¦å‡ä¸ºè¡Œä¸š top æ°´å¹³ã€‚å‡ç²‰æ£€æµ‹å’Œå—ä¼—ç”»åƒä¸‰å¹³å°ï¼ˆYT/TikTok/IGï¼‰å‡å·²è¦†ç›–ã€‚å†…éƒ¨è°ƒç”¨æˆæœ¬æä½ï¼ˆ<$0.001/æ¬¡ï¼‰ï¼Œæ— éœ€ç¬¬ä¸‰æ–¹æ•°æ®ä¾›åº”å•†ã€‚

> H4 æ˜¯å”¯ä¸€çš„å‰ç½®çº¢çº¿ï¼Œå·²é€šè¿‡éªŒè¯ã€‚H1ï¼ˆéœ€æ±‚éªŒè¯ï¼šå®‰è£…é‡å’Œä½¿ç”¨é¢‘æ¬¡ï¼‰æ”¹ä¸ºä¸Šçº¿åéªŒè¯â€”â€”éœ€è¦å…ˆæœ‰äº§å“æ‰èƒ½éªŒè¯éœ€æ±‚ã€‚

## é™„å½•

### é™„å½• Aï¼šTool Description åŸæ–‡

ä»¥ä¸‹ 5 æ®µæè¿°ç”¨äº MCP metadata çš„ `description` å­—æ®µï¼Œç›´æ¥ä» 03 é™„å½•å¤åˆ¶ã€‚

**discover_creators**
> Search and discover influencers across YouTube, TikTok, and Instagram using natural language queries. Returns a ranked list of creators with follower counts, engagement rates, authenticity flags, and estimated collaboration costs. Use this tool when a brand wants to find creators for a campaign â€” it handles search, initial screening, and basic evaluation in a single call. Supports filtering by platform, country, follower range, niche, and minimum engagement rate. TIP: If the user has searched before, check your memory for their platform and niche preferences before asking again.

**analyze_creator**
> Get a deep analysis of a specific creator's profile, including authenticity scoring, audience demographics, content performance trends, and estimated pricing. Use this tool when a brand wants to evaluate whether a creator is trustworthy and a good fit before reaching out. Accepts either a creator ID (from discover_creators results) or a direct profile URL.

**outreach_creators**
> Send personalized outreach emails to a list of creators on behalf of a brand. Generates customized email content based on the campaign brief and each creator's profile. First call returns email previews for brand approval; second call with confirm=true sends the emails and enables response tracking with automatic follow-ups. Use this when a brand is ready to contact creators they've identified. TIP: Call manage_campaigns first to get the campaign context â€” it makes the outreach email more relevant.

**negotiate**
> Negotiate collaboration pricing with a creator within the brand's budget. First provides market pricing benchmarks and a recommended negotiation strategy; then, with brand approval, conducts automated email-based negotiation. Each round of negotiation is reported back to the brand in real-time. Use this when a creator has responded to outreach and pricing discussion begins.

**manage_campaigns**
> Create and view influencer marketing campaigns. Start by creating a campaign with goals, budget, and target audience â€” this provides context for all subsequent tools. View active campaigns, collaboration history, and per-creator progress (outreach â†’ negotiation â†’ contract â†’ shipping â†’ review â†’ publish â†’ payment). Use this FIRST to set up campaign context before discovering creators, or to recall past collaboration history. Day 1 supports create + read; write operations (alerts, status updates) coming in v1.1.

### é™„å½• Bï¼šç»Ÿä¸€ Creator æ•°æ®æ¨¡å‹

```typescript
  content_count: number        // å†…å®¹æ€»æ•°

  verified: boolean            // å¹³å°è®¤è¯çŠ¶æ€

  // äº’åŠ¨æ•°æ®

    suspicious_signals: string[] // å¯ç–‘ä¿¡å·åˆ—è¡¨ï¼ˆStarter+ å¯è§ï¼‰
    verdict: "trustworthy" | "moderate" | "suspicious"  // æ‰€æœ‰å±‚çº§å¯è§
  }

  // å—ä¼—ç”»åƒï¼ˆåˆ†çº§é—¨æ§ï¼‰
  audience: {

    age_ranges: { range: string; pct: number }[] // Pro+
    gender: { female: number; male: number }     // Starter+
    interests: string[]                           // Pro+
  } | null

  // å•†ä¸šæ•°æ®
  estimated_cost: {
    min: number
    max: number
    currency: string
    basis: "market_benchmark" | "historical"
  } | null

  can_contact: boolean         // æ˜¯å¦æœ‰å¯ç”¨è”ç³»æ–¹å¼ï¼ˆStarter+ï¼‰

  // è¿‘æœŸå†…å®¹ï¼ˆanalyze è¿”å›ï¼‰
```
